package schemaversion\n2: \n3: import (\n4: \t\"context\"\n5: )\n6: \n7: // V36 migrates dashboard datasource references from legacy string format to structured UID-based objects.\n8: //\n9: // This migration addresses a critical evolution in Grafana's datasource architecture where datasource\n10: // identification shifted from potentially ambiguous display names to reliable UIDs. The original format\n11: // used string references that could break when datasources were renamed, moved between organizations,\n12: // or when multiple datasources shared similar names. This created reliability and portability issues\n13: // for dashboard sharing and automation workflows.\n14: //\n15: // The migration works by:\n16: // 1. Processing annotations, template variables, and panels (including nested panels in rows)\n17: // 2. Converting string datasource references to structured objects containing uid, type, and apiVersion\n18: // 3. Handling null/missing datasource references by setting appropriate defaults\n19: // 4. Maintaining consistency between panel and target datasource configurations\n20: // 5. Preserving special datasource types like Mixed datasources and expression queries\n21: //\n22: // This transformation provides several critical benefits:\n23: // - Eliminates datasource reference breakage when datasources are renamed\n24: // - Enables reliable dashboard export/import across different Grafana instances\n25: // - Supports advanced datasource features that require type and version information\n26: // - Prepares the schema for future datasource management enhancements\n27: // - Maintains backward compatibility while establishing a robust foundation\n28: //\n29: // The migration handles complex scenarios including:\n30: // - Panels with missing datasource configuration (set to default)\n31: // - Mixed datasource panels with heterogeneous targets\n32: // - Expression queries that reference other queries\n33: // - Template variables that depend on datasource queries\n34: // - Annotation queries from various datasource types\n35: //\n36: // Example transformations:\n37: //\n38: // Before migration (string reference):\n39: //\n40: //\tdatasource: \"prometheus-prod\"\n41: //\t// or\n42: //\tdatasource: null\n43: //\n44: // After migration (structured object):\n45: //\n46: //\tdatasource: {\n47: //\t  uid: \"prometheus-uid-123\",\n48: //\t  type: \"prometheus\",\n49: //\t  apiVersion: \"v1\"\n50: //\t}\n51: //\n52: // Before migration (panel with targets):\n53: //\n54: //\tpanel: {\n55: //\t  datasource: \"CloudWatch\",\n56: //\t  targets: [{\n57: //\t    datasource: null,\n58: //\t    refId: \"A\"\n59: //\t  }]\n60: //\t}\n61: //\n62: // After migration (consistent references):\n63: //\n64: //\tpanel: {\n65: //\t  datasource: {\n66: //\t    uid: \"cloudwatch-uid-456\",\n67: //\t    type: \"cloudwatch\",\n68: //\t    apiVersion: \"v1\"\n69: //\t  },\n70: //\t  targets: [{\n71: //\t    datasource: {\n72: //\t      uid: \"cloudwatch-uid-456\",\n73: //\t      type: \"cloudwatch\",\n74: //\t      apiVersion:
